***причуда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:причуда.html>причу́да</a> (17199)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причуда.html>причу́да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pričúda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причуда.html>причу́ды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причуда.html>причу́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причуда.html>причу́д</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>whim, whimsy, freak, caprice, fancy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:причуда.html>причу́дами</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>pričúdami</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">full of whims/freaks</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>oddity, vagary</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:причудливый.html>причу́дливый</a> (7436)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причуда.html>причу́да</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pričúda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ливый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-livyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причудливый.html>причу́дливый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pričúdlivyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>fancy, complicated</li>
<li>cute, quaint</li>
<li>bizarre, weird, peculiar <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">strangely unconventional</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> whimsical</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пришивать.html>пришива́ть</a> (22006)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пришить.html>приши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prišítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пришивать.html>пришива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prišivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пришить.html>приши́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sew on; to nail on</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to kill, to murder, to waste</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to falsely accuse of a crime, to pin an accusation</li></ol>

***пришить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пришить.html>приши́ть</a> (9973)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>шить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пришить.html>приши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prišítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пришивать.html>пришива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sew on; to nail on</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to kill, to murder, to waste</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to falsely accuse of a crime, to pin an accusation</li></ol>

***пришлый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пришлый.html>при́шлый</a> (828)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пришлый.html>при́шлый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">príšlyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>alien, foreign, nonlocal</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приют.html>прию́т</a> (9617)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приют.html>прию́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prijút</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приют.html>прию́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приют.html>прию́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приют.html>прию́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>refuge, shelter</li>
<li>asylum, orphanage</li>

***приязнь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приязнь.html>прия́знь</a> (27057)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">приꙗзнь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prijaznĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-njatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приязнь.html>прия́знь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prijáznʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приязнь.html>прия́зни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приязнь.html>прия́зни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приязнь.html>прия́зней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>friendship, friendliness, goodwill
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1984</b>,  Сергей Довлатов,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:иной.html>Ина́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:женитьба.html>жени́тьба</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:база.html>ба́зе</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обоюдный.html>обою́дной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спокойный.html>споко́йной</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:приязнь.html>прия́зни</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ženítʹba na báze obojúdnoj spokójnoj <b>prijázni</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">A marriage based on mutual calm <b>goodwill</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***приятель.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приятель.html>прия́тель</a> (1528)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">приꙗтель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prijatelĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*prijateľь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*PriH-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приятель.html>прия́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prijátelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приятель.html>прия́теля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приятель.html>прия́тели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приятель.html>прия́телей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приятельница.html>прия́тельница</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>friend, chum</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> buddy, pal, mate <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">informal address</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слушать.html>слу́шай</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:приятель.html>прия́тель</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жно</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Slúšaj, <b>prijátelʹ</b>, štó tebé núžno?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Hey, <b>mate</b>, what are you looking for?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>Ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:труп.html>труп</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:приятель.html>прия́тель</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ty trup, <b>prijátelʹ</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You're dead, <b>pal</b>!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***приятно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приятно.html>прия́тно</a> (1539)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приятный.html>прия́тный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prijátnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приятно.html>прия́тно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prijátno</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-прия́тно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)прия́тнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-прия́тно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)прия́тней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pleasantly, pleasingly, agreeably</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***проанализированный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проанализировать.html>проанализи́рованный</a> (12143)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проанализировать.html>проанализи́рованный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proanalizírovannyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проанализировать.html>проанализи́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proanalizírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
